<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:562pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><B>Note:</B> Regulation S-T Rule 
101(b)(7) only permits the submission in paper of a Form 6-K if submitted to 
furnish a report or other document that the registrant foreign private issuer 
must furnish and make public under the laws of the jurisdiction in which the 
registrant is incorporated, domiciled or legally organized (the registrant's 
&quot;home country&quot;), or under the rules of the home country exchange on 
which the registrant's securities are traded, as long as the report or other 
document is not a &nbsp;press &nbsp;release, &nbsp;is &nbsp;not required to be 
and has not been distributed to the registrant's security holders, and, if 
discussing a material event, has already been the subject of a Form 6-K 
submission or other Commission filing on EDGAR.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt"><B>President</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Dear Sirs:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>Loewen, Ondaatje, McCutcheon Limited (the 
&#147;<B>Agent</B>&#148;) understands that Kensington Resources Ltd. (the 
&#147;<B>Corporation</B>&#148;) proposes to issue (i) up to 2,307,693 flow-
through common shares in the capital of the Corporation (the &#147;<B>FT 
Shares</B>&#148;) at a price of $1.30 per FT Share, and (ii) up to 2,857,143 
units (the &#147;<B>Units</B>&#148;) at a price of $1.05 per Unit, each Unit 
being comprised of one (non flow-through) common share in the capital of the 
Corporation (each a &#147;<B>Unit Share</B>&#148;) and one-half of one common 
share purchase warrant (each a &#147;<B>Warrant</B>&#148;). Each whole Warrant 
shall be exercisable for 18 months following the Closing Date (as defined below)
and shall entitle the holder thereof to purchase one (non flow-through) common 
share in the capital of the Corporatio
n (each a &#147;<B>Warrant Share</B>&#148;) at a price per share of (A) $1.25 if
the Warrant is exercised during the first twelve months following the Closing 
Date and (B) $1.55 per share if exercised during the remaining six months prior 
to the expiration of the Warrant. . &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>The Corporation hereby appoints the Agent as the 
exclusive agent of the Corporation to solicit, on a best efforts basis, orders 
for the FT Shares and the Units, and the Agent hereby accepts such appointment 
upon and subject to the terms and conditions set out below. &nbsp;The 
Corporation agrees that the Agent is under no obligation to purchase any of the 
FT Shares or the Units.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><B>Terms and 
Conditions</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>The terms and conditions relating to the purchase and 
sale of the FT Shares and Units are as follows:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;1</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Definitions.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>The sale and issue by the Corporation of the FT Shares 
is herein referred to as the &#147;<B>FT Offering</B>&#148; and the sale and 
issue by the Corporation of the Units is herein referred to as the &#147;<B>Unit
Offering</B>&#148;. &nbsp;The FT Offering and the Unit Offering are collectively
referred to herein as the &#147;<B>Offering</B>&#148;. The date on which the 
Corporation closes the FT Offering and the Unit Offering and issues the FT 
Shares and the Units is herein referred to as the &#147;<B>Closing 
Date</B>&#148;. The time of the closing of the Offering on the Closing Date is 
herein referred to as the &#147;<B>Time</B> <B>of Closing</B>&#148;. The FT 
Shares, the Units, the Unit Shares, the Warrants, the Warrant Shares, the 
Agent&#146;s Warrants (as defined below) and the Agent&#146;s Shares (as defined
below) are collectively ref
erred to herein as the &#147;<B>Securities</B>&#148;. References herein to Unit 
Shares, Warrants and Warrant Shares shall be deemed to include Unit Shares, 
Warrants and Warrant Shares issuable by the Corporation to the Agent in 
connection with the exercise of the Agent&#146;s Unit Warrants. 
&#147;<B>Business Day</B>&#148; means any day except Saturday, Sunday or a 
statutory holiday in Toronto, Ontario.<B> Unless otherwise specified</B>, a<B>ll
dollar amounts referred to herein are Canadian dollars</B>. &nbsp;</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;2</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Offering.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Agent may offer for 
sale and sell the FT Shares and the Units to purchasers (the 
&#147;<B>Purchasers</B>&#148;) in the Provinces of British Columbia, Alberta, 
Saskatchewan, Manitoba and Ontario and in such other provinces of Canada and in 
such other jurisdictions outside of Canada as the Agent and the Corporation may 
mutually determine, in compliance with all applicable securities laws and in 
such a manner so as not to require registration thereof or filing of a 
prospectus or offering memorandum with respect thereto under such 
laws.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(2)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">If, in the opinion of the 
Agent, it is necessary, the Agent will form, manage and participate in a group 
of sub-agents to offer and sell the FT Shares and/or the Units as provided for 
hereunder. &nbsp;Each sub-agent shall be appropriately registered under the 
applicable securities laws. &nbsp;In the event that a selling group is formed, 
the Agent will:</FONT></P>

Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a)</P>

as and to the extent customary in the securities industry in Canada; 
and</FONT></P>

Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b)</P>

selling group to offer and sell the FT Shares and/or the Units, as applicable, 
on the terms set forth in this Agreement.</FONT></P>

left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(3)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-

size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation agrees to 
pay to the Agent a commission (the <B>&#147;Agent&#146;s Commission&#148;</B>) 
equal to 7% of the gross aggregate proceeds of the Offering. &nbsp;In addition, 
the Corporation shall issue to the Agent on the Closing Date (i) agent&#146;s 
share warrants (the &#147;<B>Agent&#146;s Share Warrants</B>&#148;) that shall 
entitle the Agent to purchase from the Corporation during the 18-month period 
following the Closing Date non flow-through common shares of the Corporation 
(&#147;<B>Agent&#146;s Shares</B>&#148;) equal in number to 7% of the number of 
FT Shares issued pursuant to the FT Offering at a price of $1.05 per share, and 
(ii) agent&#146;s unit warrants (the &#147;<B>Agent&#146;s Unit 
Warrants</B>&#148;) that shall entitle the Agent to purchase from the 
Corporation during the 18-month 
period following the Closing Date units equal in number to 7% of the Units 
issued pursuant to the Unit Offering at a price of $1.05 per unit, where each 
such unit shall have identical terms and conditions as the Units sold and issued
to Purchasers pursuant to the Unit Offering. &nbsp;The Agent&#146;s Share 
Warrants and the Agent&#146;s Unit Warrants are collectively referred to herein 
as the &#147;<B>Agent&#146;s Warrants</B>&#148;. </FONT></P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">Upon issuance pursuant to 
the Subscription Agreements, the FT Shares will be &#147;flow-through 
shares&#148; as defined in subsection 66(15) of the ITA and will not be 
&#147;prescribed shares&#148; for the purpose of regulation 6202.1 of the 
regulation to the ITA.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;5</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Covenants of the Corporation.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>The Corporation hereby covenants to the Agent and the 
Purchasers (and confirms, for greater certainty, that the Purchasers, in 
addition to the Agent, shall have the benefit of such covenants as if they had 
been made directly to the Purchasers under their respective Subscription 
Agreements), that:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will 
fulfil all legal requirements to permit the offering, sale and issuance of the 
FT Shares and the Units (including the Unit Shares and Warrants), the creation, 
offering, sale and issuance of the Warrants, the creation and issuance of the 
Agent&#146;s Warrants, and the issuance of the Warrant Shares and Agent&#146;s 
Shares, including, without limitation, compliance with the applicable securities
laws to enable the FT Shares and Units to be offered for sale and sold, without 
the necessity of filing a prospectus or an offering memorandum under the 
applicable securities laws of the Offering Provinces, to Purchasers through 
investment dealers or brokers registered under the applicable securities laws of
the Offering Provinces who have complied with the relevant provisions of such 
laws;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will 
obtain the necessary regulatory consents from the TSX-V to effect the Offering 
on such terms as are mutually acceptable to the Agent and the Corporation, 
acting reasonably;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will use 
its reasonable efforts to maintain the listing of the common shares of the
Corporation on the TSX-V, and arrange for the conditional listing of the FT 
Shares, the Unit Shares, the Warrant Shares and the Agent&#146;s Shares on the 
TSX-V and to maintain its status as a reporting issuer (or the equivalent) in 
British Columbia and Alberta for a period of two years from the Closing Date; 
</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">During the period from the
date hereof to the day that is 180 days after the Closing Date, the Corporation 
shall not, without the prior written consent of the Agent, such consent not to 
be unreasonably withheld, issue or enter into any agreement to issue, any 
additional common shares or financial instruments convertible or exchangeable 
into common shares of the Corporation, other than (i) for purposes of employee 
stock option or purchase plans, (ii) pursuant to the exercise of securities 
outstanding on the date hereof, and (iii) the entering into of an agreement or 
agreements, or issuing securities pursuant to an agreement or agreements, with 
J.K. Properties, Inc., Lev Leviev &amp; Company or any affiliate or associate 
thereof;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will be a 
&#147;reporting issuer&#148; as at the Time of Closing (as hereinafter defined) 
and comply with all of the requirements of Multilateral Instrument 45-102 
(&#147;<B>MI 45-102</B>&#148;) so as to permit Purchasers to be entitled to a 
four-month hold period on the FT Shares, Unit Shares and Warrants; </FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:11pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt">10</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; padding-
right:18pt; width:522pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:12pt; width:540pt; 
font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-

Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(f)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">Within the time periods 
required under the applicable securities laws of the Offering Provinces, the 
Corporation will file such documents as may be required under the applicable 
securities laws of the Offering Provinces relating to the private placement of 
the FT Shares and Units which, without limiting the generality of the foregoing,
shall include Forms 45-501F1 as prescribed by Ontario Securities Commission Rule
45-501, the form required pursuant to section 7.1(1) of Multilateral Instrument 
45-103 and any similar or comparable forms;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(g)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will (i) 
use the proceeds of the FT Offering to incur CEE on the Corporation&#146;s Fort 
&#224; la Corne property, and (ii) use the proceeds of the Unit Offering to 
finance exploration expenditures on its Fort &#224; la Corne property and any 
other mineral properties and for working capital and general corporate 
purposes;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(h)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will (i) 
incur prior to March 31, 2005 &#147;Qualifying Expenditures&#148; (as defined 
below) in such amount that enables the Corporation to renounce to the Purchasers
of the FT Shares effective December 31, 2004 in accordance with the Subscription
Agreements and the ITA, Qualifying Expenditures in an amount not less than 66 
two-thirds of the gross proceeds raised by the Corporation pursuant to the FT 
Offering (the &#147;<B>First Renunciation Amount</B>&#148;), and (ii) incur 
after March 31, 2005 and prior to December 31, 2005 Qualifying Expenditures in 
such amount that enables the Corporation to renounce to the Purchasers effective
December 31, 2005 in accordance with the Subscription Agreements and the ITA, 
Qualifying Expenditures in an amount equal to the amount of the gross proceeds 
&nbsp;rai
sed by the Corporation pursuant to the FT Offering not previously renounced 
(i.e. the remaining one-third) (the &#147;<B>Second Renunciation 
Amount</B>&#148;). &#147;<B>Qualifying Expenditures</B>&#148; refers to expenses
of the Corporation which are CEE which may be renounced by the Corporation to 
Purchasers of FT Shares pursuant to subsection 66(12.6) of the ITA;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(i)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will 
renounce, in accordance with the ITA and the Subscription Agreements relating to
the FT Offering to the Purchasers of the FT Shares (i) effective December 31, 
2004 Qualifying Expenditures in an amount equal to the First Renunciation 
Amount, and (ii) effective December 31, 2005 Qualifying Expenditures in an 
amount equal to the Second Renunciation Amount;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(j)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">All Qualifying 
Expenditures to be renounced to the Purchasers of the FT Shares pursuant to the 
applicable Subscription Agreements will be Qualifying Expenditures incurred by 
the Corporation that, but for the renunciation to such Purchasers, the 
Corporation would be entitled to deduct in computing its income for the purposes
of Part I of the ITA;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(k)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will 
maintain its status as a &#147;principal-business corporation&#148; (as defined 
in subsection 66(15) of the ITA) until at least December 31, 2006;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(l)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation will
timely (i) file all forms required under the ITA necessary to effectively 
renounce Qualifying Expenditures as per section 5(i) above, and (ii) provide to 
the Purchasers of the FT Shares all such forms and any other documentation 
required pursuant to the ITA or the Subscription Agreements so that such 
Purchasers may complete their income tax return claiming the benefit of the CEE 
renounced to them by the Corporation;;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; width:540pt;

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:12pt; width:540pt;

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-

be subject to the provisions of subsection 66(12.67) of the ITA in a manner 
which impairs its ability to renounce Qualifying Expenditures as described in 
Section 5(i) above; </FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-

Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(n)</P>

Corporation does not renounce to the Purchasers of the FT Shares (i) effective 
December 31, 2004 Qualifying Expenditures in an amount equal to the First 
Renunciation Amount, or (ii) effective December 31, 2005 Qualifying Expenditures
in an amount equal to the Second Renunciation Amount, the Corporation shall, in 
accordance with the provisions of the Subscription Agreements, indemnify each of
the Purchasers of the FT Shares as to, and pay in settlement thereof to each 
such Purchaser, an amount equal to the amount of any tax payable or that may 
become payable under the ITA (or under any corresponding provincial legislation)
by each such Purchaser as a result of such failure by the Corporation to 
renounce such Qualifying Expenditures as at such effective dates; and</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(o)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation shall not 
reduce the amount of Qualifying Expenditures renounced to the Purchasers of the 
FT Shares pursuant to subsections 66(12.6) and 66(12.66) of the ITA and, in the 
event an appropriate tax authority reduces the amount renounced to the 
Purchasers pursuant to subsection 66(12.73) of the ITA, the Corporation will, in
accordance with the provisions of the Subscription Agreements, indemnify each 
Purchaser of FT Shares as to, and pay in settlement thereof to each such 
Purchaser, an amount equal to the amount of any tax payable under the ITA (or 
under any corresponding provincial legislation) by each such Purchaser as a 
result of such reduction. </FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;6</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-

size:11pt" align=justify><B>Conditions of Closing.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-

eligible pursuant to MI 45-102 to issue securities, including the FT Shares and 
the Unit Shares and Warrants comprising the Units, having a four month

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-

Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(g)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Agent and the 
Purchasers shall have received at the Time of Closing a favourable legal opinion
of McCullough O'Connor Irwin, counsel to the Corporation and of such other 
counsel as may be required in connection with the particular opinion matters, 
addressed to the Agent and each of the Purchasers, acceptable to counsel to the 
Agent in form and substance, acting reasonably, to the effect that:</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(i)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation is a 
corporation validly subsisting under the laws of the Yukon Territory and is 
qualified to carry on business and own its assets under the laws of its 
jurisdiction of incorporation;</FONT></P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:468pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:72pt; width:468pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">Such further documentation
as may be contemplated herein or as counsel to the Agent or the applicable 
regulatory authorities may reasonably require;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>against receipt of the net proceeds of the Offering. 
&nbsp;Certificates representing the FT Shares and the Unit Shares and Warrants, 
as applicable, purchased by the Purchasers will be delivered by the Corporation 
as directed by the Agent, on behalf of the Purchasers, subject to delivery by 
the Agent to the Corporation of duly executed Subscription Agreements for 
acceptance by the Corporation. &nbsp;The Agent&#146;s Commission shall be 
deducted from the aggregate amount of the proceeds of the Offering.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;7</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Expenses.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation shall pay 
all costs and expenses incurred in connection with the Offering, including, 
without limitation, the fees and expenses of the Agent, all expenses of or 
incidental to the creation, issuance, sale or distribution of the FT Shares, the
Units and the Agent&#146;s Warrants, the fees of the Corporation&#146;s auditors
and transfer agent, and all applicable filing fees. &nbsp;The Corporation shall 
also pay the fees and disbursements of the Agent&#146;s legal counsel (including
any taxes thereon) up to a maximum of $40,000 (and, for greater certainty, 
disbursements and taxes payable in respect of the account of the Agent&#146;s 
legal counsel shall be reimbursed or paid by the Corporation but shall &nbsp;not
be subject to the foregoing cap). &nbsp;All fees and expenses of the Agent shall
be payab
le by the Corporation upon the closing of the Offering or upon the Corporation 
receiving an invoice from the Agent and shall be payable by the Corporation 
whether or not the Offering is completed.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;8</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Indemnities.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">In connection with the 
Offering, the Corporation agrees to indemnify and hold harmless the Agent, and 
each of its subsidiaries and affiliates and each of their respective directors, 
officers, employees, partners, agents, and each other person, if any, 
controlling the Agent or any of its subsidiaries or affiliates, and each 
shareholder of the Agent (collectively, the &#147;<B>Indemnified 
Parties</B>&#148; and individually, an &#147;<B>Indemnified Party</B>&#148;), 
from and against any and all losses, expenses, claims (including shareholder 
actions, derivative or otherwise), actions, damages and liabilities (other than 
loss of profits or consequential damages), joint or several, including the 
aggregate amount paid in reasonable settlement of any actions, suits, 
proceedings, investigations or claims and the reasona
ble fees and expenses of their counsel that may be incurred in advising with 
respect to and/or defending any action, suit, proceedings, investigation or 
claim that may be made or threatened against any Indemnified Party or in 
enforcing this indemnity (collectively the &#147;<B>Claims</B>&#148;) to which 
any Indemnified Party may become subject in connection with the performance of 
professional services in connection with the Offering. The Corporation also
agrees that no Indemnified Party shall have any liability (whether direct or 
indirect, in contract or tort or otherwise) to the Corporation or any person 
asserting claims on behalf of or in right of the Corporation for or in 
connection with the Offering except to the extent any losses, expenses, claims, 
actions, damages or liabilities incurred by the Corporation are determined by a 
court of competent jurisdiction in a final judgment that has become non-
appealable to have resulted primarily from the negligence, wilful misconduct or 
fraud of such Indemnified 
Party. &nbsp;The Corporation will not, without the Agent&#146;s prior written 
consent, settle, compromise, consent to the entry of any judgment in or 
otherwise seek to terminate any action, suit, proceeding, </FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:11pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt">16</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; padding-
right:18pt; width:522pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:12pt; width:540pt; 
font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-
bottom:11pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-
family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>investigation or claim in respect of 
which indemnification may be sought hereunder (whether or not any Indemnified 
Party is a party thereto) unless such settlement, compromise, consent or 
termination includes a release of each Indemnified Party from any liabilities 
arising out of such action, suit, proceeding, investigation or claim.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(2)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">Promptly after receiving 
notice of an action, suit, proceeding or claim against the Agent or any other 
Indemnified Party or receipt of notice of the commencement of any investigation 
which is based, directly or indirectly, upon any matter in respect of which 
indemnification may be sought from the Corporation, the Agent or any such other 
Indemnified Party will notify the Corporation in writing of the particulars 
thereof, provided that the omission so to notify the Corporation shall not 
relieve the Corporation of any liability which the Corporation may have to the 
Agent or any other Indemnified Party except and only to the extent that any such
delay in or failure to give notice as herein required prejudices the defence of 
such actions, suit, proceeding, claim or investigation or results in any 
material increase in
 the liability which the Corporation has under this indemnity.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(3)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation hereby 
confirms that an Indemnified Party is not required to proceed against or enforce
any other right, power, remedy or security or claim payment from or against any 
other person before making a Claim hereunder.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(4)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">To the extent that any 
Indemnified Party is not a party to this Agreement the Agent shall obtain and 
hold the right and benefit of this section in trust for and on behalf of such 
Indemnified Party.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(5)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation hereby 
consents to personal jurisdiction and service and venue in any court in which 
any claim which is subject to indemnification hereunder is brought against the 
Agent or any Indemnified Party and to the assignment of the benefit of this 
section to any Indemnified Party for the purpose of enforcement provided that 
nothing herein shall limit the Corporation's right or ability to contest the 
appropriate jurisdiction or forum for the determination of any such 
claims.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(6)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The foregoing indemnity 
shall not apply to the extent that a court of competent jurisdiction or a final 
judgment that has become non-appealable shall determine that such losses, 
expenses, claims, actions, damages or liabilities to which the Indemnified Party
may be subject were primarily caused by the negligence, wilful misconduct or 
fraud of the Indemnified Party.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(7)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">If the foregoing 
indemnification is for any reason held to be unavailable to or otherwise 
insufficient to hold harmless an Indemnified Party in respect of any losses, 
claims, damages, liabilities or expenses referred to therein, then the 
Corporation shall contribute to the aggregate amount paid or payable by such 
Indemnified Party, as incurred, as a result of any losses, claims, damages, 
liabilities or expenses referred to therein (i) in such proportion as is 
appropriate to reflect the relative benefits received by the Corporation, on the
one hand, and the Agent, on the other hand, from the Offering, or (ii) if the 
allocation provided by clause (i) above is not permitted by applicable law, in 
such proportion as is appropriate to reflect not only the relative benefits 
referred to in clause (i) above but also the 
relative fault of the Corporation, on the one hand, and the Agent, on the other 
hand, in connection with the statements or omissions or inaccuracies in the 
representations and warranties herein which resulted in such losses, claims, 
damages, liabilities or expenses, as well as any other relevant equitable 
considerations. &nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(8)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The relative benefits 
received by the Corporation, on the one hand, and the Agent, on the other hand, 
in connection with the Offering shall be deemed to be in the same respective 
proportions as </FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:11pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt">17</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; padding-
right:18pt; width:522pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:12pt; width:540pt; 
font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-
bottom:11pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-
family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>the total net proceeds from the 
Offering (before deducting expenses) received by the Corporation and the 
Agent&#146;s Commission, bear to the aggregate public offering price of the FT 
Shares and Units sold pursuant to the Offering.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(9)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The relative fault of the 
Corporation, on the one hand, and the Agent, on the other hand, shall be 
determined by reference to, among other things, whether any such untrue or 
alleged untrue statement of a material fact or omission or alleged omission to 
state a material fact or any such inaccurate or alleged inaccurate 
representation or warranty relates to information supplied by the Corporation, 
on the one hand, or the Agent, on the other hand, and the parties&#146; relative
intent, knowledge, access to information and opportunity to correct or prevent 
such statement or omission.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(10)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">Notwithstanding the 
foregoing, the Agent shall not be required to contribute any amount in excess of
the Agent&#146;s Commission. &nbsp;No person guilty of fraudulent 
misrepresentation shall be entitled to contribution from any person who was not 
guilty of such fraudulent misrepresentation. &nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(11)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation also 
agrees to reimburse the Agent for the time spent by its personnel in connection 
with any Claim at their normal <I>per diem </I>rates. &nbsp;An Indemnified Party
may retain counsel to separately represent it in the defence of a Claim, which 
shall be at the Corporation&#146;s expense if (i) the Corporation does not 
promptly assume the defence of the Claim, (ii) the Corporation agrees to 
separate representation or (iii) the Indemnified Party is advised by counsel 
that there is an actual or potential conflict in the Corporation&#146;s and the 
Indemnified Party&#146;s respective interests or additional defences are 
available to the Indemnified Party, which makes representation by the same 
counsel inappropriate.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(12)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Corporation agrees 
that in case any legal proceeding shall be brought against the Corporation
and/or the Agent by any governmental commission or regulatory authority or any 
stock exchange or other entity having regulatory authority, either domestic or 
foreign, shall investigate the Corporation and/or the Agent and any Indemnified 
Party shall be required to testify in connection therewith or shall be required 
to respond to procedures designed to discover information regarding, in 
connection with, or by reason of the performance of professional services 
rendered to the Corporation by the Agent, the Agent shall have the right, 
provided that such legal proceeding is not primarily the result of the 
Agent&#146;s negligence or wilful misconduct and is not otherwise a result of a 
more general investigation of the Ag
ent, to employ its own counsel in connection therewith, and the reasonable fees 
and expenses of such counsel as well as the reasonable costs (including an 
amount to reimburse the Agent for time spent by the personnel of the Agent in 
connection therewith) and out-of-pocket expenses incurred by the Agent&#146;s 
personnel in connection therewith shall be paid by the Corporation as they 
occur.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(13)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The obligations of the 
Corporation hereunder are in addition to any liabilities which the Corporation 
may otherwise have to the Agent or any other Indemnified Party. 
&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;9</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Termination Rights.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The Agent shall be 
entitled, at its option, to terminate all of its obligations under this 
Agreement, and the obligations of any person from whom the Agent has solicited 
an order to purchase FT Shares or Units that has executed a Subscription 
Agreement, by notice to that effect delivered to the Corporation prior to the 
Time of Closing if:</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:11pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt">18</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; padding-
right:18pt; width:522pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:12pt; width:540pt; 
font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-
bottom:11pt; padding-left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; font-
family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(a)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>the Agent is not satisfied in its sole discretion with 
its due diligence review and investigations in respect of the Corporation;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(b)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>there should occur any change, event, fact or 
circumstance (actual, contemplated or threatened) in respect of the business, 
affairs, operations, assets, liabilities (contingent or otherwise) or financial 
condition of the Corporation or any development &nbsp;that could result in such 
a change, event, fact or circumstance, or the Agent has become aware, as a 
result of its due diligence review or otherwise, of any adverse material 
information, fact or change (determined solely by the Agent) with respect to the
Corporation which had not been publicly disclosed or disclosed in writing to the
Agent prior to the date hereof, any of which, in the opinion of the Agent, as 
determined by the Agent in its sole discretion, could reasonably be expected to 
have a material adverse effect on the market price or value or the marketability
of the securiti
es of the Corporation, including the FT Shares and/or the Units; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(c)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>if any inquiry, action, suit, investigation or other 
proceeding, whether formal or informal, is commenced, threatened or publicly 
announced or any order is made under or pursuant to any statute or by any 
federal, provincial or other governmental authority, commission, board, bureau, 
agency or instrumentality (including, without limitation, the TSX-V, the British
Columbia Securities Commission or any other securities regulatory authority) in 
relation to the Corporation or the Corporation&#146;s directors or officers, 
which, in the sole opinion of the Agent operates to prevent or restrict 
materially the distribution or trading of the common shares of the Corporation, 
or materially and adversely affects or would be reasonably expected to 
materially and adversely affect the market price or value of the common shares 
of the Corporation;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(d)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>if any law or regulation is promulgated or changed 
that, in the sole opinion of the Agent, operates to prevent or restrict 
materially the distribution or trading of the common shares of the 
Corporation;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(e)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>if there should develop, occur or come into effect or 
existence any event, action, state, condition or occurrence of national or 
international consequence, any acts of hostilities or escalation thereof, or 
other calamities or crises, or any action, governmental law or regulation, 
inquiry or other occurrence, whether in any financial market or otherwise, of 
any nature whatsoever, which, in the sole opinion of the Agent materially 
adversely affects or involves or may materially adversely affect or involve the 
financial markets in Canada, the United States or elsewhere, the business or 
affairs of the Corporation, or the market price or value or marketability of the
Corporation&#146;s securities; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(f)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>the state of the financial markets or of the industry 
or markets in which the Corporation operates is or becomes such that the 
Securities cannot, in the sole opinion of the Agent, be successfully or 
profitably marketed;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(g)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>any order to cease trading the securities of the 
Corporation is made or threatened by a securities regulatory authority; 
&nbsp;or</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:11pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-size:9pt">19</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:9pt; padding-

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:12pt; width:540pt;

<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-
bottom:11pt; padding-left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; font-
family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; padding-
left:108pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman; font-size:11pt" align=justify>(h)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:108pt; width:432pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>the Agent determines that any of the representations or
warranties made by the Corporation in this Agreement is false or has become 
false.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(2)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">All terms and conditions 
of this Agreement shall be construed as conditions, and any breach or failure by
the Corporation to comply with any of such terms and conditions shall entitle 
the Agent to terminate its obligations under this Agreement by notice to that 
effect given to the Corporation at or prior to the Time of Closing. &nbsp;The 
Agent may waive, in whole or in part, or extend the time for compliance with, 
any of such terms and conditions without prejudice to their rights in respect of
any other of such terms and conditions or any other or subsequent breach or non-
compliance; provided, however, that to be binding on the Agent any such waiver 
or extension must be in writing and signed by the Agent.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(3)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">If the Agent terminates 
this Agreement pursuant to this section, there shall be no further liability on 
the part of the Agent or of the Corporation to the Agent except in respect of 
any liability that may have arisen or may thereafter arise under sections 7, 8 
or 10 hereof.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(4)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The right of the Agent to 
terminate its obligations under this Agreement is in addition to such other 
remedies as it has or may have in respect of any default, act or failure to act 
of the Corporation in respect of any of the matters contemplated by this 
Agreement.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;10</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Alternative Transaction.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">In the event that the 
Corporation withdraws from or terminates either of the FT Offering or the Unit 
Offering prior to the Time of Closing as the result of entering into an 
&#147;Alternative Transaction&#148; (as defined below) which is entered into by 
the Corporation or any of its shareholders without the prior written consent of 
the Agent prior to November 23, 2004, the Corporation shall pay (i) the 
Agent&#146;s Commission that would be otherwise payable pursuant to the terms 
hereof assuming the FT Offering had closed and raised gross proceeds of 
$2,000,000 and assuming the Unit Offering had closed and raised gross proceeds 
of $2,000,000, and (ii) the Agent&#146;s expenses as provided for in section 7. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-
left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Book 
Antiqua; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(2)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; padding-
left:36pt; width:504pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Book Antiqua; font-
size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">For the purposes hereof, 
an &#147;<B>Alternative Transaction</B>&#148; means the issuance of securities 
of the Corporation in excess of 10% of the total value or number of securities 
outstanding on a fully diluted basis, but does not include the issuance of 
securities as contemplated in paragraphs 5(d)(i), (ii) and (iii) above, or a 
merger, amalgamation, arrangement, reorganization, take-over bid, insider bid, 
joint venture, or the sale or exchange of all or substantially all of the assets
or any such similar transaction involving or relating to the 
Corporation.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;11</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Right of First Refusal.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>The Corporation agrees that, upon the completion of the
Offering, the Agent shall be entitled to act as the lead member of an investment
banking syndicate in connection with any brokered equity financing undertaken by
the Corporation during the period of one year from the Closing Date. All members
of any such investment banking syndicate will be subject to approval by the 
Corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:-13pt; width:540pt; 
line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>Section&#160;12</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-
indent:72pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify><B>Breach of Agreement.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" align=justify>Any breach of, or failure by the Corporation to comply 
with, any term or condition of this Agreement shall entitle the Agent, on behalf
of the Purchasers, to terminate its obligations to purchase the FT Shares or 
Units, as applicable, by notice to that effect given to the Corporation prior to
the Time of Closing, and there shall be no further liability on the part of the 
Corporation or such Agent except in respect of any liability which may have 
arisen or may thereafter arise under sections 7, 8 or 10 hereof. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-
indent:36pt; width:540pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><BR>

time for compliance with, any terms and conditions without prejudice to its

align=justify><B>Section&#160;13</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:3.65pt; text-

size:11pt" align=justify><B>Confidentiality.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:72pt; margin-bottom:11pt; text-

concerning the business and affairs of the Corporation will be treated and held 
in confidence by the Agent and its directors, officers, employees, advisors and 
agents and will not be disclosed or used other than in connection with the 
performance by the Agent of its duties hereunder without the Corporation&#146;s 
prior written consent except as required by law (including applicable securities
laws) or legal process or by any competent administrative authority and, in such
event, only after prior consultation with the Corporation. The Agent&#146;s 
obligations under this section will terminate on the first anniversary of the 
Closing Date.</P>

notice is faxed; if such notice is sent by mail, it shall be effective four

Corporation contained herein or contained in any document submitted pursuant to 
this Agreement or in connection with the purchase of the FT Shares and/or the 
Units shall survive the purchase of such securities for a period of three years 
from the Time of Closing by the Purchasers and shall continue in full force and 
effect unaffected by any subsequent disposition or conversion of any of such 
securities.</P>

time to time represent other diamond exploration companies in corporate finance 
matters and the Corporation, for greater certainty, hereby confirms its 
understanding that the Agent may act on such other matters with other companies 
prior to, concurrent with or subsequent to the Offering.</P>
